 Cordiac surgery is also called open heart surgery
 open heart surgery do tarah kii hoti he
 One is when the veins of the heart get blocked and the other when there is a problem in the valves of the heart
 aaie jaanate hai ams main kaise kii jaati he cardiyak surgery
 Bypass surgery is done when the veins of the heart are blocked
 bypass surgery main chaati main chira lagaakar andar se ek dhamni jise internal thoracic artery kehete hai kaa oparation kiya jaataa he
 It first takes the arm or leg vein and uses it as a carrier tube
 yah tabhi kiya jaataa he jab hriday kii teenon mukhya dhamniyon main samasya hoti he
